<resp>None</resp>< Review>
Lifesaver!!! Best kept secret at SFO. I had an unexpected overnight lay over due to bad weather. I was traveling alone, and I called every nearby airport hotel that offered shuttle service. Due to COVID that service was unavailable, or only for essential workers. I found this hidden gem on Yelp. It looks like a normal sundries store, but they have three modest rooms with private bathrooms and shower rooms. It was expensive, but was really clean with very helpful and friendly staff. Heads up - overnight hours are 10pm-6am. There are only 3 rooms, so definitely CALL AHEAD!< /Review>

< review>
Had a 8 hour workday plus a 4 hour flight, and was about to catch another 20-hour long flight. Seeing such a facility in SFO was very welcome.

Take note that the price is steep (25 USD for 30 mins) and the shower room isn't the most conducive for that activity (as someone mentioned - no separation of dry/wet areas).

That said - you will get the essential toileteries and towels needed for a proper shower and you will definitely be refreshed.

I'd recommend it if you've got a very long flight looming ahead/you don't have lounge access.</review>

I rented my Jucy Van for the first time and had a great experience.  I'll start with the end.... I left $200 under the drivers side floor mat and did not realize until later that night.  I called first thing the next day, the manager Gerald went right to the van while on the phone and was able to recover it - so you know your dealing with honest people - THANK YOU.

Registration on the Web was easy.... the cost included 100 miles a day, linens and kitchen supplies..... so your good to go with no add ons needed.

I flew into San Francisco and followed the Jucy Website instructions and took the BART.... very easy.... even easier/faster flying in/out of Oakland.

When I arrived they quickly and thoroughly took me through the paper work and van.

I was off, while the van had a lot of miles on it and was clearly used.... it was in good shape and drove well.

I'm 6 feet and slept comfortably..... as it was a bit cold I slept in the van but that penthouse looked even nicer.

Drop off outside of my knucklehead move was also very efficient.

Thanks Jucy and Gerald - I look forward to future Jucy journeys!!</Text>

<date>1456766680007</date>< review>
I almost never write reviews (they're usually positive), but if I could give zero stars for wasting my time, I would.

While the rental was fine, dealing with their backoffice incompetence has cost me hours of time. Two months after the rental, they sent us a message saying that there had been a Golden Gate Bridge Toll Violation. I responded that we had been no where near the Golden Gate Bridge. They responded, "oh, sorry, wrong violation" and said it was a Metro ExpressLane violation. I responded that we had a FastTrak and that we did not recall being in an ExpressLane - please send me details. Nothing... (other than a $50 administrative processing fee on my credit card which I disputed).

Fast forward another month and the Metro ExpressLane violation shows up and it's in Los Angeles -- about 300 miles from where we were and it was not the vehicle we rented. 1.5hrs later - after calling Jucy (and getting someone in Australia who was clueless, talking to LA Metro and Bay Area Fastrak), I finally got someone on the line at Bay Area Fastrak and am paying the $2.50 toll even though it wasn't our vehicle.

If I hadn't disputed the admin fee and provided my Fastrak account number, the fees alone would have been $75. All because Jucy couldn't get the right license plate number associated with a contract. Thanks for the waste of time, Jucy! I would have rented again, but this leaves a bitter taste and the lack of customer support is appalling.</review>

<rating>1</rating>< review>
Eating way too much pizza, I spend a minimum of $40 per week at this location. I will NEVER order from here again as of now. The shift manager, so he says, was very rude to me when I called in about being double charged. I was double charged Sunday, it is now Thursday, and this is the first time I have even been able to get thru to talk to someone, and the treatment I get is uncalled for. Tye, the young man I talked to, wanted to get me off the phone, said nothing but "ok" in a rude tone that told me he could care less, didn't want to answer my questions, and then proceeded to hang up on me.  I again, I will NEVER go here again.  I will give round table or dominos my money on a regular basis from now on!<//review>

<Pics>None< /Pics><user_id>103938964872255733492</user_id><GmapID>0x809ace6b020ee7a7:0xb7201a84a66446a9< /GmapID>< review>
I had my very first "Pizza Guys" pizza for dinner today.  Using a coupon and handing over $23 dollars, I got an extra large four topping pizza, and a pint of ice cream.  Not bad I gotta say.

As for the taste and pitting it against other pizza makers that charge approximately the same, I'd say it's much  better than Pappa Johns, also better than Pizza Hut's greasy excuse, which by default makes it also better than BJ's (aka: the brewery) greasy-oil dripping concoction.  To use a boxing term, this pizza punches above its weight, meaning it will KO (...that means knock-out...) Round Table Pizza, specifically the one next to Bel Air Supermarket near Florin Rd & I-5 Fwy.  All-in-all, it's not bad.  Is it better than Marri's near Disneyland and New Yorks Best Pizzaria in Mission Viejo, well no it's not, but then again, those places are more expensive.  In racing terms, will it open a one car lead against California Pizza Kitchen, according to my taste buds, not a chance in...   ...well, you know.  Then again, Pizza Guys is a take-out only maker, not a sit-in and dine brick-and-mortar business like CPK, so that comparison is not exactly fair.  How about I put it this way, it is not the Bruce Lee of pizzas, but then again it's not the Ralph Macchio (...think Karate Kid if you got no imagination... :D ) of pizzas either.  Generally, it's solid.< /review>

Went there today for father's day and it was a mess. I truly regret dropping $100 on such bad customer service. My group consisted of four people. Me, my wife, mom and dad. To start the food took way too long. I had ordered two shrimp cocktails, which you would think those would have been delivered first maybe about 15 minutes into the order. Anyways, my dad gets his food first 30 minutes after ordering. Then about ten minutes later my wife and I get our food and about ten more minutes my mom.  It took about 50 minutes before my mom could get a plate of menudo. Then to top it off my wife's order was wrong so we had to send it back. My food came with tortillas which I never got and quite frankly we had been waiting so long for our food that we got filled with the tortilla chips and salsa.

Now it was busy so I have some sympathy but not much. The bottom line is we are still customers and that should not be an excuse. I've been there once on a regular business day and the service was ok not great ok. So like I said I know the potential for them to give great customer service is their.
